@ $mol_mem
    agc(next?: string): string {
      if (next !== undefined) {
        const response = $radar_fetch.post( '/uccmscp_settings_manager/upload_settings', {
          "image_mode" : {
            "temperature": next,
            "type": this.adjustment()
          }
        }) as {
          "data": {
            "image_mode": {
              "success": boolean,
              "value": {
                "brightness": number,
                "contrast": number,
                "temperature": "room0"|"low"|"room1"|"high",
                "type": "manual"|"auto"
              }
            }
          }
        }
        this.updateBrightnessAndContrast(response)
        return next
      }
      return this.default_agc()
    }

    default_agc() {
      return this.initSettings().image_mode.temperature
    }

    private updateBrightnessAndContrast(postResponse: {
      "data": {
        "image_mode": {
          "success": boolean,
          "value": {
            "brightness": number,
            "contrast": number,
            "temperature": "room0"|"low"|"room1"|"high",
            "type": "manual"|"auto"
          }
        }
      }
    }) {

      if (this.isAgcModeIsNormal() ) {
        this.brightness(postResponse.data.image_mode.value.brightness + 32)
      } else {
        this.brightness(postResponse.data.image_mode.value.brightness)
      }

      this.contrast(postResponse.data.image_mode.value.contrast)
    }


    @ $mol_mem
    brightness(next?: number): number {
      console.log(`brightness(${next})`)
      return next ?? this.default_brightness();
    }

    default_brightness() {
      let brightness = this.initSettings().image_mode.brightness
      if (this.isAgcModeIsNormal()) {
        brightness += 32
      }
      return brightness
    }
